CREATE TABLE rave_adm0030 (
    study varchar(15)  NOT  NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    instn integer4     NOT  NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    patid integer4     NOT  NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    event varchar(50)  NOT  NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    eventRepeat varchar(100) WITH NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    formRepeat integer2     WITH NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    groupRepeat integer2     WITH NULL NOT DEFAULT,
    version integer4 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepdate timestamp(0) WITH TIME ZONE WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepdate_raw varchar(11) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    week integer2 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    week_raw varchar(4) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    stepno integer1 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    stepno_raw varchar(2) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptxrecyn varchar(3) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptxrecyn_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptxrecyn_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptxstopdate timestamp(0) WITH TIME ZONE WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptxstopdate_raw varchar(11) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepreasoncode varchar(72) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepreasoncode_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepreasoncode_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepspecify varchar(30) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    offstepreason varchar(140) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    finalstepyn varchar(3) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    finalstepyn_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    finalstepyn_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    newstepyn varchar(3) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    newstepyn_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    newstepyn_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    newstep varchar(6) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    newstep_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    newstep_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptype varchar(38) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptype_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    steptype_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    commentyn varchar(3) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    commentyn_decode varchar(200) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    commentyn_cl varchar(50) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    comment140 varchar(140) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    sysdat integer4 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    sysdat_raw varchar(9) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    dchng integer4 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    dchng_raw varchar(9) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    review integer1 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    review_raw varchar(2) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    seqno integer1 WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    seqno_raw varchar(3) WITH NULL WITH DEFAULT NULL,
    mincreated timestamp(3) with time zone with null with default null,
    maxupdated timestamp(3) with time zone with null with default null,
    savets     timestamp(3) with time zone with null with default null,
    changeTime timestamp(3) with time zone not  null not  default
); \p\g
MODIFY rave_adm0030 TO btree UNIQUE ON study, patid, event, eventRepeat, formRepeat, groupRepeat; \p\g
GRANT SELECT ON rave_adm0030 TO GROUP alldata; \p\g
GRANT SELECT ON rave_adm0030 TO GROUP rando; \p\g
GRANT SELECT ON rave_adm0030 TO GROUP statdata; \p\g
GRANT SELECT ON rave_adm0030 TO GROUP ldms; \p\g
GRANT SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE ON rave_adm0030 TO javauser; \p\g
